ZX_VRAM:4000             ;             - (built at run-time)

SCRATCH:5C08             ;
SCRATCH:5C08             ; table of objects (40 max)
SCRATCH:5C08             ; - 00,01 player sprites (00=bottom, 01=top)
SCRATCH:5C08             ; - 02,03 special object sprites
SCRATCH:5C08             ; - 04-39 background, then foreground
SCRATCH:5C08             ;
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +0 graphic_no.
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +1 x (center)
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +2 y (center)
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +3 z (bottom)
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +4 width (X radius)
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +5 depth (Y radius)
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +6 height
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +7 flags
SCRATCH:5C08             ;    - 7=vflip sprite
SCRATCH:5C08             ;    - 6=hflip sprite
SCRATCH:5C08             ;    - 5=wipe
SCRATCH:5C08             ;    - 4=draw
SCRATCH:5C08             ;    - 3=auto-adjust near arches (player only)
SCRATCH:5C08             ;    - 2=moveable
SCRATCH:5C08             ;    - 1=ignore in 3D calculations
SCRATCH:5C08             ;    - 0=is near arch (player only)
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +8 screen
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +9 dX
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +10 dY
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +11 dZ
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +12 counter and flags
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 7-4=counter when entering screen
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 3=jumping
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 2=Z out-of-bounds
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 1=Y out-of-bounds
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 0=X out-of-bounds
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +13 per-object info/flags
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - direction and counters for looking, turning
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 7=deadly if object hits player
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 6=dead
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 5=deadly if player hits object
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 4=(not used)
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 3=triggered (dropping, collapsing blocks)
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 2=up (bouncing ball), dropping (spiked ball)
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 1=north (NS fire)
SCRATCH:5C08             ;     - 0=east (WE fire, EW guard), just dropped (spec objs)
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +14 d_x_adj
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +15 d_y_adj
SCRATCH:5C08             ; +16-17 ptr object table entry or tmp player graphic_no

SCRATCH:5C08             ; +19 pixel Y adjustment

RAM:AFC7             update_sprite_loop:                                             ; init stack

RAM:AFCA 21 BC 5B                    ld      hl, #fire_seed
RAM:AFCD 34                          inc     (hl)
RAM:AFCE 21 E4 AF                    ld      hl, #ret_from_tbl_jp

RAM:AFD5
RAM:AFD5             jump_to_upd_object:                                             ; sprite graphic to render
RAM:AFD5 DD 6E 00                    ld      l, 0(ix)
RAM:AFD8 01 96 B0                    ld      bc, #upd_sprite_jmp_tbl
RAM:AFDB
RAM:AFDB             jump_to_tbl_entry:
RAM:AFDB 26 00                       ld      h, #0
RAM:AFDD 29                          add     hl, hl                                  ; word offset
RAM:AFDE 09                          add     hl, bc                                  ; get ptr jump entry
RAM:AFDF 7E                          ld      a, (hl)
RAM:AFE0 23                          inc     hl
RAM:AFE1 66                          ld      h, (hl)
RAM:AFE2 6F                          ld      l, a                                    ; HL=jump address
RAM:AFE3 E9                          jp      (hl)                                    ; go
RAM:AFE3             ; END OF FUNCTION CHUNK FOR lose_life

RAM:AFE4             ret_from_tbl_jp:

RAM:AFE6 4F                          ld      c, a
RAM:AFE7 3A A5 5B                    ld      a, (seed_3)
RAM:AFEA 81                          add     a, c

RAM:AFF5 E1                          pop     hl

RAM:AFF9 A7                          and     a

RAM:AFFC 30 02                       jr      NC, loc_B000                            ; yes, exit
RAM:AFFE 18 C7                       jr      update_sprite_loop                      ; loop

RAM:B2DA             play_note:
RAM:B2DA E6 3F                       and     #0x3F ; '?'                             ; note
RAM:B2DC 28 3E                       jr      Z, snd_delay
RAM:B2DE 6F                          ld      l, a
RAM:B2DF 26 00                       ld      h, #0
RAM:B2E1 29                          add     hl, hl                                  ; HL=2A
RAM:B2E2 CD F2 D4                    call    add_HL_A                                ; HL=3A
RAM:B2E5 01 32 B3                    ld      bc, #freq_tbl                           ; frequency table
RAM:B2E8 09                          add     hl, bc                                  ; ptr to entry
RAM:B2E9 46                          ld      b, (hl)                                 ; loop cnt LSB
RAM:B2EA 23                          inc     hl
RAM:B2EB 4E                          ld      c, (hl)                                 ; loop cnt MSB
RAM:B2EC 23                          inc     hl
RAM:B2ED 6E                          ld      l, (hl)                                 ; duration LSB
RAM:B2EE 26 00                       ld      h, #0
RAM:B2F0 1A                          ld      a, (de)                                 ; note & duration MSB
RAM:B2F1 07                          rlca
RAM:B2F2 07                          rlca
RAM:B2F3 E6 03                       and     #3
RAM:B2F5 3C                          inc     a                                       ; duration MSB
RAM:B2F6 D5                          push    de
RAM:B2F7 5D                          ld      e, l
RAM:B2F8 54                          ld      d, h                                    ; HL,DE=duration LSB
RAM:B2F9
RAM:B2F9             calc_duration:

RAM:B2FA 28 03                       jr      Z, loc_B2FF
RAM:B2FC 19                          add     hl, de
RAM:B2FD 18 FA                       jr      calc_duration                           ; calc 16-bit duration (HL)

RAM:B2FF D1                          pop     de

RAM:BC18             count_screens:
RAM:BC18 C5                          push    bc
RAM:BC19 7E                          ld      a, (hl)
RAM:BC1A 23                          inc     hl
RAM:BC1B
RAM:BC1B             loc_BC1B:
RAM:BC1B 0F                          rrca
RAM:BC1C 30 01                       jr      NC, loc_BC1F

RAM:BC1F
RAM:BC1F             loc_BC1F:
RAM:BC1F 10 FA                       djnz    loc_BC1B
RAM:BC21 C1                          pop     bc
RAM:BC22 0D                          dec     c                                       ; done all screens?
RAM:BC23 20 F3                       jr      NZ, count_screens                       ; no, loop
RAM:BC25 7B                          ld      a, e
RAM:BC26 3D                          dec     a                                       ; -1? don't count 1st room?

RAM:BC2A 3A BB 5B                    ld      a, (objects_put_in_cauldron)

RAM:BC2F 83                          add     a, e
RAM:BC30 5F                          ld      e, a
RAM:BC31 01 1A A4                    ld      bc, #0xA41A                             ; 0.64102 * (128 + 14*2) = 99.999%
RAM:BC34 21 00 00                    ld      hl, #0
RAM:BC37 AF                          xor     a
RAM:BC38
RAM:BC38             loc_BC38:
RAM:BC38 09                          add     hl, bc
RAM:BC39 CE 00                       adc     a, #0
RAM:BC3B 27                          daa
RAM:BC3C 1D                          dec     e
RAM:BC3D 20 F9                       jr      NZ, loc_BC38                            ; calculate percentage complete (BCD)
RAM:BC3F 01 28 00                    ld      bc, #0x28 ; '('                         ; $A410*156 = $63FFD8+$28 = $640000
RAM:BC42 09                          add     hl, bc
RAM:BC43 CE 00                       adc     a, #0
RAM:BC45 27                          daa                                             ; fix rounding to 100%

RAM:BC4E 32 C9 5B                    ld      (percent_msw), a                        ; store most significant BCD digit
RAM:BC51 21 E6 E4                    ld      hl, # vidbuf+0xBF3
RAM:BC54 11 C9 5B                    ld      de, #percent_msw
RAM:BC57 06 01                       ld      b, #1                                   ; 1 pair = 2 digits
RAM:BC59 1A                          ld      a, (de)
RAM:BC5A A7                          and     a                                       ; 100%?
RAM:BC5B 28 04                       jr      Z, loc_BC61                             ; no, skip
RAM:BC5D 04                          inc     b                                       ; 2 pair = 4 digits
RAM:BC5E C3 C0 BC                    jp      print_BCD_lsd

RAM:BCC9 C9                          ret

RAM:BD15             loc_BD15:                                                       ; reset flashing attribute

RAM:BD23
RAM:BD23             menu_loop:
RAM:BD23 CD B3 BE                    call    display_menu
RAM:BD26 11 53 B2                    ld      de, #menu_tune
RAM:BD29 CD B6 B2                    call    play_audio_wait_key
RAM:BD2C 3E F7                       ld      a, #0xF7 ; ''                          ; 1,2,3,4,5
RAM:BD2E CD F7 B5                    call    read_port
RAM:BD31 5F                          ld      e, a                                    ; store keybd status
RAM:BD32 3A A4 5B                    ld      a, (user_input_method)
RAM:BD35 32 A6 5B                    ld      (old_input_method), a
RAM:BD38 CB 43                       bit     0, e                                    ; '1' (keyboard)?
RAM:BD3A 28 02                       jr      Z, check_for_kempston_joystick          ; no, skip
RAM:BD3C E6 F9                       and     #0xF9 ; ''                             ; mask off (bits 2,1)
RAM:BD3E
RAM:BD3E             check_for_kempston_joystick:                                    ; '2' (Kempston Joystick)?
RAM:BD3E CB 4B                       bit     1, e
RAM:BD40 28 04                       jr      Z, check_for_cursor_joystick            ; no, skip
RAM:BD42 E6 F9                       and     #0xF9 ; ''                             ; mask off (bits 2,1)
RAM:BD44 F6 02                       or      #2                                      ; set bit 1
RAM:BD46
RAM:BD46             check_for_cursor_joystick:                                      ; '3' (Cursor Joystick)?
RAM:BD46 CB 53                       bit     2, e
RAM:BD48 28 04                       jr      Z, check_for_interface_ii               ; no, skip
RAM:BD4A E6 F9                       and     #0xF9 ; ''                             ; mask off (bits 2,1)
RAM:BD4C F6 04                       or      #4                                      ; set bit 2
RAM:BD4E
RAM:BD4E             check_for_interface_ii:                                         ; '4' (Interface II)?
RAM:BD4E CB 5B                       bit     3, e
RAM:BD50 28 02                       jr      Z, check_for_directional_control        ; no, skip
RAM:BD52 F6 06                       or      #6                                      ; set bits 1,2
RAM:BD54
RAM:BD54             check_for_directional_control:                                  ; store
RAM:BD54 32 A4 5B                    ld      (user_input_method), a
RAM:BD57 21 D2 5B                    ld      hl, #debounce_5
RAM:BD5A CB 63                       bit     4, e                                    ; '5' (directional control)?
RAM:BD5C 28 27                       jr      Z, clr_debounce                         ; no, skip
RAM:BD5E CB 46                       bit     0, (hl)                                 ; was pressed last time?
RAM:BD60 20 0A                       jr      NZ, check_for_start_game                ; yes, skip
RAM:BD62 CB C6                       set     0, (hl)                                 ; set debounce
RAM:BD64 3A A4 5B                    ld      a, (user_input_method)
RAM:BD67 EE 08                       xor     #8                                      ; toggle directional
RAM:BD69 32 A4 5B                    ld      (user_input_method), a
RAM:BD6C
RAM:BD6C             check_for_start_game:
RAM:BD6C 21 A6 5B                    ld      hl, #old_input_method
RAM:BD6F BE                          cp      (hl)                                    ; changed input method?
RAM:BD70 C4 A3 B4                    call    NZ, toggle_audio_hw_x16                 ; yes
RAM:BD73 3E EF                       ld      a, #0xEF ; ''                          ; 0,9,8,7,6
RAM:BD75 CD F7 B5                    call    read_port
RAM:BD78 CB 47                       bit     0, a                                    ; '0' (Start Game)?
RAM:BD7A C0                          ret     NZ                                      ; yes, exit
RAM:BD7B 21 A0 5B                    ld      hl, #seed_1
RAM:BD7E 34                          inc     (hl)                                    ; remember when BASIC games did this?
RAM:BD7F CD 89 BD                    call    flash_menu
RAM:BD82 C3 23 BD                    jp      menu_loop
RAM:BD85             ; ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
RAM:BD85
RAM:BD85             clr_debounce:
RAM:BD85 CB 86                       res     0, (hl)
RAM:BD87 18 E3                       jr      check_for_start_game                    ; continue
RAM:BD87             ; End of function do_menu_selection
RAM:BD87
RAM:BD89

RAM:BD89
RAM:BD89             flash_menu:
RAM:BD89 21 A3 BD                    ld      hl, # menu_colours+1
RAM:BD8C 3A A4 5B                    ld      a, (user_input_method)
RAM:BD8F 0F                          rrca
RAM:BD90 E6 03                       and     #3                                      ; keybd/joystick bits only
RAM:BD92 06 04                       ld      b, #4
RAM:BD94 CD A3 BE                    call    toggle_selected
RAM:BD97 CB BE                       res     7, (hl)
RAM:BD99 3A A4 5B                    ld      a, (user_input_method)
RAM:BD9C E6 08                       and     #8                                      ; directional only
RAM:BD9E C8                          ret     Z
RAM:BD9F CB FE                       set     7, (hl)
RAM:BDA1 C9                          ret
RAM:BDA1             ; End of function flash_menu

RAM:BE31             print_text_single_colour:

RAM:BE3A CD 11 D8                    call    calc_vidbuf_addr

RAM:BE3F 3A B6 5B                    ld      a, (tmp_attrib)

RAM:BE45             print_text_std_font:

RAM:BE4C
RAM:BE4C             print_text:
RAM:BE4C C1                          pop     bc
RAM:BE4D C5                          push    bc
RAM:BE4E CD 11 D8                    call    calc_vidbuf_addr
RAM:BE51 69                          ld      l, c
RAM:BE52 60                          ld      h, b                                    ; HL = bitmap buffer address
RAM:BE53 1A                          ld      a, (de)                                 ; attribute
RAM:BE54 08                          ex      af, af'
RAM:BE55 13                          inc     de                                      ; ptr first character
RAM:BE56
RAM:BE56             loc_BE56:
RAM:BE56 D9                          exx
RAM:BE57 E1                          pop     hl                                      ; HL = Y,X
RAM:BE58 D5                          push    de
RAM:BE59 CD 48 D8                    call    calc_attrib_addr
RAM:BE5C 6B                          ld      l, e
RAM:BE5D 62                          ld      h, d                                    ; HL = attribute memory address
RAM:BE5E D1                          pop     de
RAM:BE5F
RAM:BE5F             loc_BE5F:
RAM:BE5F D9                          exx
RAM:BE60 1A                          ld      a, (de)                                 ; next character
RAM:BE61 CB 7F                       bit     7, a                                    ; done?
RAM:BE63 20 0D                       jr      NZ, loc_BE72                            ; yes, skip
RAM:BE65 D5                          push    de
RAM:BE66 CD 7F BE                    call    print_8x8                               ; display a character
RAM:BE69 D1                          pop     de
RAM:BE6A 13                          inc     de
RAM:BE6B D9                          exx
RAM:BE6C 08                          ex      af, af'
RAM:BE6D 77                          ld      (hl), a                                 ; store attribute
RAM:BE6E 2C                          inc     l                                       ; next attribute addrsess
RAM:BE6F 08                          ex      af, af'
RAM:BE70 18 ED                       jr      loc_BE5F                                ; loop until message done
RAM:BE72             ; ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
RAM:BE72
RAM:BE72             loc_BE72:                                                       ; mask off end-of-message bit
RAM:BE72 E6 7F                       and     #0x7F ; ''
RAM:BE74 D5                          push    de
RAM:BE75 CD 7F BE                    call    print_8x8                               ; display a character
RAM:BE78 D1                          pop     de
RAM:BE79 13                          inc     de
RAM:BE7A D9                          exx
RAM:BE7B 08                          ex      af, af'
RAM:BE7C 77                          ld      (hl), a                                 ; store attribute
RAM:BE7D D9                          exx
RAM:BE7E C9                          ret
RAM:BE7E             ; End of function print_text_std_font
RAM:BE7E
RAM:BE7F
RAM:BE7F             ; =============== S U B R O U T I N E =======================================
RAM:BE7F
RAM:BE7F
RAM:BE7F             print_8x8:
RAM:BE7F C5                          push    bc
RAM:BE80 D5                          push    de
RAM:BE81 E5                          push    hl
RAM:BE82 6F                          ld      l, a
RAM:BE83 26 00                       ld      h, #0                                   ; HL = character
RAM:BE85 29                          add     hl, hl
RAM:BE86 29                          add     hl, hl
RAM:BE87 29                          add     hl, hl                                  ; calculate offset into font data
RAM:BE88 ED 5B C7 5B                 ld      de, (gfxbase_8x8)
RAM:BE8C 19                          add     hl, de                                  ; calculate address of font data
RAM:BE8D EB                          ex      de, hl                                  ; DE = font data
RAM:BE8E E1                          pop     hl
RAM:BE8F 06 08                       ld      b, #8                                   ; # bytes (lines) to display
RAM:BE91
RAM:BE91             loc_BE91:                                                       ; get font data byte
RAM:BE91 1A                          ld      a, (de)
RAM:BE92 77                          ld      (hl), a                                 ; store in video/buffer memory
RAM:BE93 13                          inc     de                                      ; next font data byte
RAM:BE94 C5                          push    bc
RAM:BE95 01 E0 FF                    ld      bc, #0xFFE0                             ; next video/buffer line
RAM:BE98 09                          add     hl, bc
RAM:BE99 C1                          pop     bc
RAM:BE9A 10 F5                       djnz    loc_BE91                                ; loop until done character
RAM:BE9C D1                          pop     de
RAM:BE9D 01 01 01                    ld      bc, #0x101
RAM:BEA0 09                          add     hl, bc                                  ; video/buffer address for next character
RAM:BEA1 C1                          pop     bc
RAM:BEA2 C9                          ret
RAM:BEA2             ; End of function print_8x8

RAM:BF37             ; sparkles (object in cauldron)
RAM:BF37
RAM:BF37             upd_185_187:
RAM:BF37 DD 6E 10                    ld      l, 16(ix)
RAM:BF3A DD 66 11                    ld      h, 17(ix)
RAM:BF3D             ;
RAM:BF3D             ;  BUG: this routine is primarily for special objects
RAM:BF3D             ;       when dropped into cauldron etc (disappear)
RAM:BF3D             ;  BUT: when the collapsing block disappears, the
RAM:BF3D             ;       graphic_no is set to 184, which is then
RAM:BF3D             ;       incremented to 185, and we end up here.
RAM:BF3D             ;  ONLY: there's no special object entry (HL=0)
RAM:BF3D             ;
RAM:BF3D             ;  So it zaps [$0000] which is ROM
RAM:BF3D             ;  - and harmless on the ZX Spectrum.
RAM:BF3D             ;
RAM:BF3D             ; BUG VERIFIED! on the Spectrum under MESS
RAM:BF3D             ;
RAM:BF3D 36 00                       ld      (hl), #0                                ; zap graphic_no in special_objs_tbl
RAM:BF3F             ; last death sparkle
RAM:BF3F
RAM:BF3F             upd_119:

RAM:BF4E             display_objects:

RAM:BF59
RAM:BF59             display_object:
RAM:BF59 C5                          push    bc
RAM:BF5A E5                          push    hl
RAM:BF5B 78                          ld      a, b
RAM:BF5C ED 44                       neg
RAM:BF5E C6 03                       add     a, #3                                   ; (~b+3)
RAM:BF60 CB 27                       sla     a
RAM:BF62 CB 27                       sla     a
RAM:BF64 CB 27                       sla     a                                       ; =(~b+3)*8
RAM:BF66 4F                          ld      c, a
RAM:BF67 CB 27                       sla     a                                       ; (~b+3)*16
RAM:BF69 81                          add     a, c                                    ; =(~b+3)*24
RAM:BF6A C6 10                       add     a, #16                                  ; =(~b+3)*24+16
RAM:BF6C DD 77 1A                    ld      26(ix), a                               ; pixel X
RAM:BF6F DD 36 1B 00                 ld      27(ix), #0                              ; pixel Y
RAM:BF73 DD 4E 1A                    ld      c, 26(ix)                               ; pixel X
RAM:BF76 DD 46 1B                    ld      b, 27(ix)                               ; pixel Y
RAM:BF79 E5                          push    hl                                      ; ptr object
RAM:BF7A CD 11 D8                    call    calc_vidbuf_addr
RAM:BF7D 69                          ld      l, c
RAM:BF7E 60                          ld      h, b
RAM:BF7F 01 18 03                    ld      bc, #0x318                              ; width=3, height=24
RAM:BF82 AF                          xor     a                                       ; fill byte = 0
RAM:BF83 CD 15 C5                    call    fill_window                             ; wipe 24x24 pixel area
RAM:BF86 E1                          pop     hl                                      ; ptr object
RAM:BF87 7E                          ld      a, (hl)                                 ; object (sprite index)
RAM:BF88 A7                          and     a                                       ; null?
RAM:BF89 28 06                       jr      Z, loc_BF91                             ; yes, skip
RAM:BF8B DD 77 00                    ld      0(ix), a                                ; sprite index
RAM:BF8E CD 18 D7                    call    print_sprite
RAM:BF91
RAM:BF91             loc_BF91:                                                       ; pixel X
RAM:BF91 DD 4E 1A                    ld      c, 26(ix)
RAM:BF94 DD 46 1B                    ld      b, 27(ix)                               ; pixel Y
RAM:BF97 CD 26 D8                    call    calc_vram_addr
RAM:BF9A CD 11 D8                    call    calc_vidbuf_addr
RAM:BF9D 69                          ld      l, c
RAM:BF9E 60                          ld      h, b
RAM:BF9F 01 03 18                    ld      bc, #0x1803                             ; lines=24, bytes=3
RAM:BFA2 CD 7C D6                    call    blit_to_screen
RAM:BFA5 E1                          pop     hl                                      ; ptr object
RAM:BFA6 C1                          pop     bc
RAM:BFA7 C5                          push    bc
RAM:BFA8 E5                          push    hl                                      ; ptr object
RAM:BFA9 7E                          ld      a, (hl)                                 ; object (sprite index)
RAM:BFAA E6 0F                       and     #0xF
RAM:BFAC 5F                          ld      e, a
RAM:BFAD 16 00                       ld      d, #0
RAM:BFAF 21 D3 BF                    ld      hl, #object_attributes
RAM:BFB2 19                          add     hl, de
RAM:BFB3 4E                          ld      c, (hl)                                 ; get fill byte entry
RAM:BFB4 DD 6E 1A                    ld      l, 26(ix)                               ; pixel X
RAM:BFB7 DD 7E 1B                    ld      a, 27(ix)                               ; pixel Y
RAM:BFBA C6 17                       add     a, #23
RAM:BFBC 67                          ld      h, a
RAM:BFBD CD 48 D8                    call    calc_attrib_addr
RAM:BFC0 EB                          ex      de, hl
RAM:BFC1 79                          ld      a, c                                    ; fill byte
RAM:BFC2 01 03 03                    ld      bc, #0x303                              ; width=3, height=3
RAM:BFC5 CD 15 C5                    call    fill_window
RAM:BFC8 E1                          pop     hl                                      ; ptr object
RAM:BFC9 C1                          pop     bc                                      ; object count
RAM:BFCA 23                          inc     hl
RAM:BFCB 23                          inc     hl
RAM:BFCC 23                          inc     hl
RAM:BFCD 23                          inc     hl                                      ; next entry (4 bytes)
RAM:BFCE 10 89                       djnz    display_object                          ; loop through all objects
RAM:BFD0 DD E1                       pop     ix
RAM:BFD2 C9                          ret
RAM:BFD2             ; End of function display_objects

RAM:C591             ; updates special objects table with current data (coords etc)
RAM:C591             ; - traverses special_objs_here table
RAM:C591             ; - writes to special_objs_tbl
RAM:C591             ;
RAM:C591             ; Another bug related to ptr special_objs_tbl
RAM:C591             ; - the cauldron bubbles are inserted in the object table
RAM:C591             ;   dynamically when you enter the room. This routine checks
RAM:C591             ;   the graphic_no for null, but (again) not the ptr
RAM:C591             ;   and (again) writes to ROM @$0000
RAM:C591             ; * VERIFIED on the ZX Spectrum emulator!
RAM:C591             ;
RAM:C591
RAM:C591             ; =============== S U B R O U T I N E =======================================
RAM:C591
RAM:C591
RAM:C591             update_special_objs:
RAM:C591 FD 21 48 5C                 ld      iy, #special_objs_here
RAM:C595
RAM:C595             loc_C595:                                                       ; get graphic no.
RAM:C595 FD 7E 00                    ld      a, 0(iy)
RAM:C598 A7                          and     a                                       ; null?
RAM:C599 28 1C                       jr      Z, loc_C5B7                             ; yes, skip
RAM:C59B FD 5E 10                    ld      e, 16(iy)
RAM:C59E FD 56 11                    ld      d, 17(iy)                               ; DE=ptr object table entry
RAM:C5A1 FD 7E 00                    ld      a, 0(iy)                                ; get graphic no.
RAM:C5A4 12                          ld      (de), a                                 ; store
RAM:C5A5 13                          inc     de
RAM:C5A6 13                          inc     de
RAM:C5A7 13                          inc     de
RAM:C5A8 13                          inc     de
RAM:C5A9 13                          inc     de
RAM:C5AA FD E5                       push    iy
RAM:C5AC E1                          pop     hl                                      ; HL=object in 'here' table
RAM:C5AD 23                          inc     hl                                      ; ptr x
RAM:C5AE 01 03 00                    ld      bc, #3                                  ; 3 bytes
RAM:C5B1 ED B0                       ldir                                            ; copy x, y, z
RAM:C5B3 FD 7E 08                    ld      a, 8(iy)                                ; screen
RAM:C5B6 12                          ld      (de), a                                 ; store as current
RAM:C5B7
RAM:C5B7             loc_C5B7:
RAM:C5B7 01 20 00                    ld      bc, #32
RAM:C5BA FD 09                       add     iy, bc                                  ; next entry in 'here' table
RAM:C5BC FD E5                       push    iy
RAM:C5BE E1                          pop     hl
RAM:C5BF 01 88 5C                    ld      bc, #other_objs_here                    ; end of table
RAM:C5C2 A7                          and     a
RAM:C5C3 ED 42                       sbc     hl, bc                                  ; past end of table?
RAM:C5C5 38 CE                       jr      C, loc_C595                             ; no, loop
RAM:C5C7 C9                          ret

RAM:CFD1
RAM:CFD1             loc_CFD1:                                                       ; graphic_no
RAM:CFD1 7E                          ld      a, (hl)
RAM:CFD2 23                          inc     hl
RAM:CFD3 FE FF                       cp      #0xFF                                   ; end of list?
RAM:CFD5 CA C3 CE                    jp      Z, process_remaining_objs               ; yes, exit
RAM:CFD8 B9                          cp      c                                       ; what we're looking for?
RAM:CFD9 20 F6                       jr      NZ, loc_CFD1                            ; no, loop
RAM:CFDB FD E5                       push    iy
RAM:CFDD DD E1                       pop     ix                                      ; obj#2=obj#1
RAM:CFDF 18 22                       jr      render_obj
RAM:CFE1             ; ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
RAM:CFE1
RAM:CFE1             objs_coincide:                                                  ; obj#1 graphic no.
RAM:CFE1 DD 7E 00                    ld      a, 0(ix)
RAM:CFE4 D6 60                       sub     #0x60 ; '`'
RAM:CFE6 FE 07                       cp      #7                                      ; special object?
RAM:CFE8 30 06                       jr      NC, loc_CFF0                            ; no, skip
RAM:CFEA DD 36 00 BB                 ld      0(ix), #187                             ; set to twinkle sprite
RAM:CFEE 18 0D                       jr      loc_CFFD
RAM:CFF0             ; ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
RAM:CFF0
RAM:CFF0             loc_CFF0:                                                       ; object #2 graphic no.
RAM:CFF0 FD 7E 00                    ld      a, 0(iy)
RAM:CFF3 D6 60                       sub     #0x60 ; '`'
RAM:CFF5 FE 07                       cp      #7                                      ; special object?
RAM:CFF7 30 04                       jr      NC, loc_CFFD                            ; no, skip
RAM:CFF9 FD 36 00 BB                 ld      0(iy), #187                             ; set to twinkle sprite
RAM:CFFD
RAM:CFFD             loc_CFFD:                                                       ; continue
RAM:CFFD C3 DB CE                    jp      loc_CEDB

RAM:D000             render_obj_no1:

RAM:D003
RAM:D003             render_obj:                                                     ; back to entry we're searching for
RAM:D003 2B                          dec     hl
RAM:D004 CB FE                       set     7, (hl)                                 ; flag as rendered
RAM:D006 3E FF                       ld      a, #0xFF
RAM:D008 32 1A D0                    ld      (render_list), a                        ; set entry to empty
RAM:D00B 21 BE 5B                    ld      hl, #rendered_objs_cnt
RAM:D00E 34                          inc     (hl)

RAM:D012 C3 C3 CE                    jp      process_remaining_objs                  ; restart processing again

RAM:D043 C5                          push    bc

RAM:D046
RAM:D046             loc_D046:

RAM:D047 CB 11                       rl      c                                       ; reverse bit order
RAM:D049 10 FB                       djnz    loc_D046                                ; loop thru all bits
RAM:D04B 79                          ld      a, c

RAM:D3CF             find_screen:                                                    ; get location ID

RAM:D3D1 DD BE 08                    cp      8(ix)                                   ; same as player (current) screen?
RAM:D3D4 28 1A                       jr      Z, found_screen                         ; yes, exit

RAM:D865             vflip_sprite_data:                                              ; sprite data address
